select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '06/01/2019' and '06/30/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '06/01/2019' and '06/30/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc

[2019-07-01 15:32:54.000000 192.130.74.20  - [query->JOLALDE] ] SELECT sum(a.subtotal) subtotal , sum(a.descuento) descuento, sum( a.TotImpuesto) impuesto , sum(a.monto_flete) envio , sum( (a.total+a.monto_flete))  total   FROM  VentasDiariasCMACST a INNER JOIN MDocumentos  b ON a.doc = b.codtipodoc   WHERE a.fechafac between '06/01/2019' AND '06/30/2019'  AND  a.statfact=3 and  coditems  in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ) and cod_subgrupo ='CEL MADRE'   

[2019-07-01 15:32:54.000000 192.130.74.20  - [query->JOLALDE] ] 
select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '06/01/2019' and '06/30/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
